#;Q1=The most difficult thing was choosing a strategy. That is, I can either remain consistent by selecting folders based on the speaker's perspective, or by selecting folders based on my perspective. Thinking about my own conversations, I would tend to say, "Give me the folder on *your* right", or "Give me the folder in the front *of you*". Given that, I decided to assume that the speaker was asking me to choose folders based on my perspective, so once I made that determination, the task was not difficult.;Q3=Yes;Q2=I assumed that I was not connected to a real-life person, so it did not feel like I was connected.
